  LOAD: 'load',\n    IDLE: 'idle',\n}\n\nfunction Alarm(name, type, subprop, tagprop) {\n    this.name = name;\n    this.type = type;\n    this.subproperty = subprop;\n    this.tagproperty = tagprop;\n    this.ontime = 0;\n    this.offtime = 0;\n    this.acktime = 0;\n    this.status = AlarmStatusEnum.VOID;\n    this.lastcheck = 0;\n    this.toremove = false;\n    this.userack;\n\n    this.getId = function () {\n        return this.name + '^~^' + this.type;\n    }\n\n    this.check = function (time, dt, value) {\n        if (this.lastcheck + (this.subproperty.checkdelay * TimeMultiplier) > time) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        this.lastcheck = time;\n        this.toremove = false;\n        var onrange = (value >= this.subproperty.min && value <= this.subproperty.max);\n        switch(this.status) {\n            case AlarmStatusEnum.VOID: {\n                //  check to activate\n                if (!onrange) {\n                    return false;\n                } else if (!this.ontime) {\n                    this.ontime = dt;\n                    return false;\n                }\n                if (this.ontime + (this.subproperty.timedelay * TimeMultiplier) < time) {\n                    this.status = AlarmStatusEnum.ON;\n                    return true;\n                }\n            }\n            case this.acktime) {\n                        this.toRemove();\n                    } \n                    return true;\n                }\n                if (this.acktime) {\n                    this.status = AlarmStatusEnum.ACK;\n                    return true;\n                }\n                return false;\n            }\n            case AlarmStatusEnum.OFF: {\n                // check to reactivate\n                if (onrange) {\n                    this.status = AlarmStatusEnum.ON;\n                    this.acktime = 0;\n\t\t\t\t\tthis.offtime = 0;\n                    this.ontime = time;\n                    this.userack = '';\n                    return true;\n                }\n                // remove if acknowledged\n                if (this.acktime || this.type === AlarmsTypes.ACTION) {\n                    this.toRemove();\n                    return true;\n                }\n                return false;\n            }\n            case      }\n                        }\n                        _checkWorking(false);\n                    });\n                } catch {\n                    _checkWorking(false);\n                }\n            } else {\n                _checkWorking(false);\n            }\n        } else {\n            _emitStatus('connect-busy');                    \n        }\n\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Load requestItemsMap[data.tags[id].address].push(data.tags[id]);   \n                } else {\n                    requestItemsMap[data.tags[id].address] = [data.tags[id]];\n                }\n            }\n            logger.info(`'${data.name}' data loaded (${count})`, true);\n        } catch (error) {\n            logger.error(`'${data.name}' load error! ${error}`);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return Objects (Tags) values array { id: <name>, value: <value>, type: <type> }\n     */\n    this.getValues = function () {\n        return data.tags;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return Tag value {                  logger.error(`'${data.name}' _readProperty error! ${error}`);\n                    }\n                }\n                Promise.all(readfnc).then(results => {\n                    if {\n            if (askey) {\n                return formatAddress('000000', token);\n            } \n            return ModbusMemoryAddress.CoilStatus;\n        } else if (address < ModbusMemoryAddress.InputRegisters) {\n            if (askey) {\n                return formatAddress(ModbusMemoryAddress.DigitalInputs, token);\n            }\n            return Number.parseFloat(divisor);\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(error);\n        }\n        return value;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return the Items that are wit refTagToTopics[item.value] = { value: null, topics: [] };\n                            }\n                            refTagToTopics[item.value].topics.push(data.tags[key]);\n                        } else if (item.type === 'value') {\n                            // raw data (not depending from other tag)\n                            item.value = '';\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            logger.info(`'${data.name}' data loaded (${count})`, true);\n        } catch (error) {\n            logger.error(`'${data.name}' load error! ${error}`);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return Topic value { id: <name>, value: <value>, ts: <timestamp> }\n     */\n    this.getValue = function (id) {\n        if (varsValue[id]) {\n            return { id: id, value: varsValue[id].value, ts: lastTimestampValue };\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return Topics values array { id: <name>, value: <value>, type: <type> }\n     */\n    this.getValues = function () {\n        return data.tags;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the Topic value, publish to broker (coming from frontend)\n     */\n    this.setValue = function (tagid, value) {\n        if (client && client.connected) {\n            var tag = data.tags[tagid];\n            if (tag) {\n                if (tag.options) {\n                    if (tag.options.pubs) {\n                        for (const item of tag.options.pubs) {\n                            if (item.type === 'value') {\n                                item.value = value;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    } else if (tag.options.subs && tag.options.subs.includes(tag.memaddress)) {\n                        tag.value = value;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (tag.type === 'raw') {\n                    tag['value'] = value;\n                }\n                tag.changed = true;\n                _publishValues([tag]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return Device status Connected/Disconnected 'connect-off', 'connect-ok', 'connect-error'\n     */\n    this.getStatus = function () {\n        return lastStatus;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return Topic property, not used (Topics don't have property)\n     */\n    this.getTagProperty = function (topic) {\n        if (data.tags[topic]) {\n            let prop = { id: topic, name: data.tags[topic].name, type: data.tags[topic].type };\n            return prop;\n        } else {\n            return null;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a subscription to receive Topics value\n     */\n    var _createSubscription = function () {\n        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n            var topics = Object.values(data.tags).map(t => t.address);\n            _mapTopicsAddress(Object.values(data.tags));\n            if (topics && topics.length > 0) {\n                client.subscribe(topics, function (err) {\n                    if (err) {\n                        reject(err);\n                    } else {\n                        client.on('message', function (topicAddr, msg, pkt) {\n                            if (topicsMap[topicAddr]) {\n                                for (var i = 0; i < topicsMap[topicAddr].length; i++) {\n                            data.tags[id].timestamp = Date.now();\n                                    data.tags[id].changed = oldvalue !== data.tags[id].value;\n                                    if (data.tags[id].type === 'json' && data.tags[id].options && data.tags[id].options.subs && data.tags[id].memaddress) {\n                                        try {\n   }\n                                    }\n                                }\n                            }\n                        });\n                        resolve();\n                    }\n                });\n            } else {\n                resolve();\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create the receiver of change tag value for the dependency in payload\n     */\n    var _createRefPublishReceiver = function () {\n        events.on('tag-value:changed', function (event) {\n            try {\n                if (memoryTagToPublish.has(event.id)) {\n                    // for topic with raw data (not depending from other tag)\n                    var oldValue = memoryTagToPublish.get(event.id);\n                    memoryTagToPublish.set(event.id, refTagToTopics[event.id].topics.length; i++) {\n                                _publishValues([refTagToTopics[event.id].topics[i]]);\n                            }\n                        }\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(error);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n    /**\n     * Map the topics to address (path)\n     * @param {*} topics \n     */\n    var _mapTopicsAddress = function (topics) {\n        var tmap = {};\n        for (const topic of topics) {\n            if (tmap[topic.address]) {\n                tmap[topic.address].push(topic);\n            } else {\n                tmap[topic.address] = [topic];\n            }\n        }\n        topicsMap = tmap;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Clear local Topics   return false;\n            }\n        }\n        working = check;\n        overloading = 0;\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Reset the timeout by browse the Topics, 10 seconds to _publishValues = function (tags) {\n        for (const key of Object.keys(tags)) {\n            try {\n                // publish only tags with pubs and value changed\n                if                      var value = '';\n                        if (item.type === 'tag' && item.value) {        // tag from other devices\n                            if (memoryTagToPublish.has(item.value)) {\n                                value = memoryTagToPublish.get(item.value);\n                            }\n                        } else if (item.type === 'timestamp') {         // timestamp to add in tag with value\n                            value = new Date().toISOString();\n                        } else if (item.type === 'value') {             // tag created in mqtt device as value\n                            value = item.value;\n                        } else {    // item.type === 'static'\n                            value = item.value;\n             topicTopuplish[0] = value;\n                        }\n                    }\n                    // payloand\n                    if (tags[key].type === 'json') {\n client.publish(tags[key].address, Object.values(topicTopuplish)[0].toString());\n                    }\n                } else if (tags[key].type === 'json' && tags[key].options && tags[key].value.toString());\n                    tags[key].value = null;\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(error);\n            }\n        }\n '${prjstorage.TableType.ALARMS}' ${error}`);\n                                callback(error);\n                            });\n                        },\n                        // step 3 get notifications\n                        function (callback) {\n                            getNotifications().then(notifications => {\n                                data.notifications = notifications;\n                                callback();\n                            }).catch(function (error) {\n                                logger.error(`project.prjstorage-failed-to-load! '${prjstorage.TableType.NOTIFICATIONS}' ${error}`);\n                                callback(error);\n                            }); \n                        },\n                        // step 4 get scripts\n                        function (callback) {\n                            getScripts().then(scripts => {\n                                data.scripts = scripts;\n                                callback();\n                            }).catch(function (error) {\n                                logger.error(`project.prjstorage-failed-to-load! '${prjstorage.TableType.SCRIPTS}' ${error}`);\n                                callback(error);\n                            });\n                        },\n                        // step 5 get reports\n                        function (callback) {\n                            getReports().then(reports => {\n                                data.reports = reports;\n                                callback();\n                            }).catch(function (error) {\n                                logger.error(`project.prjstorage-failed-to-load! '${prjstorage.TableType.REPORTS}' ${error}`);\n                                callback(error);\n                            }); \n                        }\n                    ],\n                    async function (err) {\n                        if (err) {\n                            reject(err);\n                        } else {\n                            await _mergeDefaultConfig();\n                            resolve();\n                        }\n                    });\n                }).catch(function (error) {\n                    logger.error(`project.prjstorage-failed-to-load! '${prjstorage.TableType.DEVICES}' ${error}`);\n                    reject(error);\n                });\n            }).catch(function (error) {\n                logger.error(`project.prjstorage-failed-to-load! '${prjstorage.TableType.VIEWS}' ${error}`);\n                reject(error);\n            });\n        }).catch(function (error) {\n            logger.error(`project.prjstorage-failed-to-load! '${prjstorage.TableType.GENERAL}' ${error}`);\n            reject(error);\n        });\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Save the value in project storage\n * First set the value in local data, then save in storage\n * @param {*} cmd \n * @param {*} data \n */\nfunction setProjectData(cmd, value) {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        try {\n            var toremove = false;\n            var section = { table: '', name: '', value: value };\n            switch (cmd) {\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.SetView: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.VIEWS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                setView(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.DelView: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.VIEWS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                toremove = removeView(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.HmiLayout: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.GENERAL;\n                section.name = cmd;\n                setHmiLayout(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.SetDevice: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.DEVICES;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                setDevice(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.DelDevice: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.DEVICES;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                toremove = removeDevice(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.Charts: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.GENERAL;\n                section.name = cmd;\n                setCharts(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.Graphs: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.GENERAL;\n                section.name = cmd;\n                setGraphs(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.SetText: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.TEXTS;\n                section.name = value.name;\n                setText(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.DelText: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.TEXTS;\n                section.name = value.name;\n                toremove = removeText(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.SetAlarm: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.ALARMS;\n                section.name = value.name;\n                setAlarm(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.DelAlarm: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.ALARMS;\n                section.name = value.name;\n                toremove = removeAlarm(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.SetNotification: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.NOTIFICATIONS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                setNotification(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.DelNotification: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.NOTIFICATIONS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                toremove = removeNotification(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.SetScript: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.SCRIPTS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                setScript(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.DelScript: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.SCRIPTS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                toremove = removeScript(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.SetReport: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.REPORTS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                setReport(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            case ProjectDataCmdType.DelReport: {\n                section.table = prjstorage.TableType.REPORTS;\n                section.name = value.id;\n                toremove = removeReport(value);\n            \n            break;\n            }\n            default: {\n                logger.error(`prjstorage.setdata failed! '${section.table}'`);\n                reject('prjstorage.failed-to-setdata: Command not found!');    \n            }\n            }\n            if (toremove) {\n                prjstorage.deleteSection(section).then(result => {\n                    resolve(true);\n                }).catch(function (error) {\n                    logger.error(`prjstorage.deletedata failed! '${section.table}'`);\n                    reject(error);\n                });\n            } else {\n                prjstorage.setSection(section).then(result => {\n                    resolve(true);\n                }).catch(function (error) {\n                    logger.error(`prjstorage.setdata failed! '${section.table}'`);\n                    reject(error);\n                });\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            reject(error);\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Set or add if not exist (check with view.id) the View in Project\n * @param {*} view \n */\nfunction setView(view) {\n    var pos = -1;\n    for (var i = 0; i < data.hmi.views.length; i++) {\n        if (data.hmi.views[i].id === view.id) {\n            pos = i;\n        }\n    }\n    if (pos >= 0) {\n        data.hmi.views[pos] = view;\n    } else {\n        data.hmi.views.push(view);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Remove the View from Project\n * @param {*} view \n */\nfunction removeView(view) {\n    var pos = -1;\n    for (var i = 0; i < data.hmi.views.length; i++) {\n        if (data.hmi.views[i].id === view.id) {\n            data.hmi.views.splice(i, 1);\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set Device to local data\n * @param {*} device \n * @param {*} merge merge with exist (tags)\n */\nfunction setDevice(device, merge) {\n    if (merge && data.devices[device.id]) {\n        device.enabled = data.devices[device.id].enabled;\n        data.devices[device.id] = {...data.devices[device.id], ...device};\n    } else {\n        data.devices[device.id] = device;\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Remove Device from local data\n * @param {*} device \n */\nfunction removeDevice(device) {\n    delete data.devices[device.id];\n    return true;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set HMI Layout to local data\n * @param {*} layout \n */\nfunction setHmiLayout(layout) {\n    data.hmi.layout = layout;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set Charts  \n * @param {*} charts \n */\nfunction setCharts(charts) {\n    data.charts = charts;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set Graphs  \n * @param {*} graphs \n */\n function setGraphs(graphs) {\n    data.graphs = graphs;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set or add if not exist (check with taxt.name) the Text in Project\n * @param {*} text \n */\nfunction setText(text) {\n    if (!data.texts) {\n        data.texts = [];\n    }\n    var pos = -1;\n    for (var i = 0; i < data.texts.length; i++) {\n        if (data.texts[i].name === text.name) {\n            pos = i;\n        }\n    }\n    if (pos >= 0) {\n        data.texts[pos] = text;\n    } else {\n        data.texts.push(text);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Remove the Text from Project\n * @param {*} text \n */\nfunction removeText(text) {\n    if (data.texts) {\n        var pos = -1;\n        for (var i = 0; i < data.texts.length; i++) {\n            if (data.texts[i].name === text.name) {\n                data.texts.splice(i, 1);\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set or add if not exist (check with alarm.name) the Alarm in Project\n * @param {*} alarm \n */\nfunction setAlarm(alarm) {\n    if (!data.alarms) {\n        data.alarms = [];\n    }\n    var pos = -1;\n    for (var i = 0; i < data.alarms.length; i++) {\n            if (data.alarms[i].name === alarm.name) {\n                data.alarms.splice(i, 1);\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set or add if not exist (check with notification.id) the Notification in Project\n * @param {*} notification \n */\n function setNotification(notification) {\n    if (!data.notifications) {\n        data.notifications = [];\n    }\n    var pos = -1;\n    for (var i = 0; i < data.notifications.length; i++) {\n        if (data.notifications[i].id === notification.id) {\n            pos = i;\n        }\n    }\n    if (pos >= 0) {\n        data.notifications[pos] = notification;\n    } else {\n        data.notifications.push(notification);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Remove the Notification from Project\n * @param {*} notification \n */\nfunction removeNotification(notification) {\n    if (data.notifications) {\n        var pos = -1;\n        for (var i = 0; i < data.notifications.length; i++) {\n            if (data.notifications[i].id === notification.id) {\n                data.notifications.splice(i, 1);\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set or add if not exist (check with script.id) the Script in Project\n * @param {*} script \n */\n function setScript(script) {\n    if (!data.scripts) {\n        data.scripts = [];\n    }\n    var pos = -1;\n    for (var i = 0; i < data.scripts.length; i++) {\n        if (data.scripts[i].id === script.id) {\n            pos = i;\n        }\n    }\n    if (pos >= 0) {\n        data.scripts[pos] = script;\n    } else {\n        data.scripts.push(script);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Remove the Script from Project\n * @param {*} script \n */\n function removeScript(script) {\n    if (data.scripts) {\n        var pos = -1;\n        for (var i = 0; i < data.scripts.length; i++) {\n            if (data.scripts[i].id === script.id) {\n                data.scripts.splice(i, 1);\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set or add if not exist (check with report.id) the Report in Project\n * @param {*} report \n */\n function setReport(report) {\n    if (!data.reports) {\n        data.reports = [];\n    }\n    var pos = -1;\n    for (var i = 0; i < data.reports.length; i++) {\n        if (data.reports[i].id === report.id) {\n            pos = i;\n        }\n    }\n    if (pos >= 0) {\n        data.reports[pos] = report;\n    } else {\n        data.reports.push(report);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Remove the Report from Project\n * @param {*} script \n */\n function removeReport(report) {\n    if (data.reports) {\n        var pos = -1;\n        for (var i = 0; i < data.reports.length; i++) {\n            if (data.reports[i].id === report.id) {\n                data.reports.splice(i, 1);\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the project data in accordance with autorization\n */\nfunction getProject(userId, userGroups) {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        const pdata = _filterProjectGroups(userGroups);\n        resolve(pdata);\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Set the new Project, clear all from database and add the new content\n * @param {*} prjcontent \n */\nfunction setProject(prjcontent) {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        try {\n            prjstorage.clearAll().then(result => {\n                var scs = [];\n                for (const key of Object.keys(prjcontent)) {\n                    switch (key) {\n                    case 'devices': {\n                        // devices\n                        var devices = prjcontent[key];\n                        if (devices) {\n                            for (const device of Object.values(prjcontent[key])) {\n                                scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.DEVICES, name: device.id, value: device });\n                            }\n                        }\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    case 'hmi': {\n                        // hmi\n                        var hmi = prjcontent[key];\n                        if (hmi) {\n                            for (const hk of Object.keys(hmi)) {\n                                if (hk === 'views') {\n                                    // views\n                                    if (hmi[hk] && hmi[hk].length > 0) {\n                                        for (var i = 0; i < hmi[hk].length; i++) {\n                                            var view = hmi[hk][i];\n                                            scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.VIEWS, name: view.id, value: view });\n                                        }\n                                    }\n                                } else {\n                                    // layout\n                                    scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.GENERAL, name: hk, value: hmi[hk] });\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    case 'server': {\n                        // server\n                        scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.DEVICES, name: key, value: prjcontent[key] });\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    case 'texts': {\n                        // texts\n                        var texts = prjcontent[key];\n                        if (texts && texts.length > 0) {\n                            for (var i = 0; i < texts.length; i++) {\n                                scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.TEXTS, name: texts[i].name, value: texts[i] });\n                            }\n                        }\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    case 'alarms': {\n                        // alarms\n                        var alarms = prjcontent[key];\n                        if (alarms && alarms.length > 0) {\n                            for (var i = 0; i < alarms.length; i++) {\n                                scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.ALARMS, name: alarms[i].name, value: alarms[i] });\n                            }\n                        }\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    case 'notifications': {\n                        // notifications\n                        var notifications = prjcontent[key];\n                        if (notifications && notifications.length > 0) {\n                            for (var i = 0; i < notifications.length; i++) {\n                                scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.NOTIFICATIONS, name: notifications[i].id, value: notifications[i] });\n                            }\n                        }\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    case 'scripts': {\n                        // scripts\n                        var scripts = prjcontent[key];\n                        if (scripts && scripts.length > 0) {\n                            for (var i = 0; i < scripts.length; i++) {\n                                scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.SCRIPTS, name: scripts[i].id, value: scripts[i] });\n                            }\n                        }\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    case 'reports': {\n                        // reports\n                        var reports = prjcontent[key];\n                        if (reports && reports.length > 0) {\n                            for (var i = 0; i < reports.length; i++) {\n                                scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.REPORTS, name: reports[i].id, value: reports[i] });\n                            }\n                        }\n                    \n                    break;\n                    }\n                    default: {\n                        // charts, graphs, version\n                        scs.push({ table: prjstorage.TableType.GENERAL, name: key, value: prjcontent[key] });\n                    }\n                    }\n                }\n                prjstorage.setSections(scs).then(() => {\n                    logger.info(`project.prjstorage.set-project successfull!`, true);\n                    resolve(true);\n                }).catch(function (error) {\n                    reject(error);\n                });\n            }).catch(function (error) {\n                logger.error(`project.prjstorage.clear failed! '${error}'`);\n                reject(error);\n            });\n        } catch {\n            reject();\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Return Devices list\n */\nfunction getDevices() {\n    return data.devices;\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the device property\n */\nfunction getDeviceProperty(query) {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        if (query.query === 'security') {\n            prjstorage.getSection(prjstorage.TableType.DEVICESSECURITY, query.name).then(drows => {\n                if (drows.length > 0) {\n                    resolve(drows[0]);\n                } else {\n                    resolve();\n                }\n            }).catch(function (error) {\n                logger.error(`project.prjstorage.getdevice-property failed! '${prjstorage.TableType.DEVICESSECURITY} ${error}'`);\n                reject(error);\n            });\n        } else {\n            reject();\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the texts \n */\nfunction getTexts() {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        prjstorage.getSection(prjstorage.TableType.TEXTS).then(drows => {\n            if (drows.length > 0) {\n                var texts = [];\n                for (const drow of drows) {\n                    texts.push(JSON.parse(drow.value));\n                }\n                resolve(texts);\n            } else {\n                resolve();\n            }\n        }).catch(function (error) {\n            logger.error(`project.prjstorage.get-texts failed! '${prjstorage.TableType.TEXTS} ${error}'`);\n            reject(error);\n        });\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the alarms \n */\nfunction getAlarms() {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        prjstorage.getSection(prjstorage.TableType.ALARMS).then(drows => {\n            if (drows.length > 0) {\n                var alarms = [];\n                for (const drow of drows) {\n                    alarms.push(JSON.parse(drow.value));\n                }\n                resolve(alarms);\n            } else {\n                resolve();\n            }\n        }).catch(function (error) {\n            logger.error(`project.prjstorage.get-alarms failed! '${prjstorage.TableType.ALARMS} ${error}'`);\n            reject(error);\n        });\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the notifications \n */\n function getNotifications() {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        prjstorage.getSection(prjstorage.TableType.NOTIFICATIONS).then(drows => {\n            if (drows.length > 0) {\n                var notifications = [];\n                for (const drow of drows) {\n                    notifications.push(JSON.parse(drow.value));\n                }\n                resolve(notifications);\n            } else {\n                resolve();\n            }\n        }).catch(function (error) {\n            logger.error(`project.prjstorage.get-notifications failed! '${prjstorage.TableType.NOTIFICATIONS} ${error}'`);\n            reject(error);\n        });\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the scripts \n */\n function getScripts() {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        prjstorage.getSection(prjstorage.TableType.SCRIPTS).then(drows => {\n            if (drows.length > 0) {\n                var scripts = [];\n                for (const drow of drows) {\n                    scripts.push(JSON.parse(drow.value));\n                }\n                resolve(scripts);\n            } else {\n                resolve();\n            }\n        }).catch(function (error) {\n            logger.error(`project.prjstorage.get-scripts failed! '${prjstorage.TableType.SCRIPTS} ${error}'`);\n            reject(error);\n        });\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the reports \n */\n function getReports() {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        prjstorage.getSection(prjstorage.TableType.REPORTS).then(drows => {\n            if (drows.length > 0) {\n                var reports = [];\n                for (const drow of drows) {\n                    reports.push(JSON.parse(drow.value));\n                }\n                resolve(reports);\n            } else {\n                resolve();\n            }\n        }).catch(function (error) {\n            logger.error(`project.prjstorage.get-reports failed! '${prjstorage.TableType.REPORTS} ${error}'`);\n            reject(error);\n        });\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Set the device property\n */\nfunction setDeviceProperty(query) {\n    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n        if (query.query === 'security') {\n            prjstorage.setSection({ table: prjstorage.TableType.DEVICESSECURITY, name: query.name, value: query.value }).then(() => {\n                resolve();\n            }).catch(function (error) {\n                logger.error(`project.prjstorage.setdevice-property failed! '${prjstorage.TableType.DEVICESSECURITY} ${error}'`);\n                reject(error);\n            });\n        } else {\n            reject();\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n/**\n * Return Project demo from file\n */\nfunction getProjectDemo() {\n    var demoProject = path.join(settings.appDir, 'project.demo.fuxap');\n    return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(demoProject, 'utf8'));\n}\n\nfunction _filterProjectGroups(groups) {\n    var result = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data));// = { devices: {}, hmi: { views: [] } };\n    var admin = (groups === -1 || groups === 255) ? true : false;\n    if (!admin) {\n        // from device remove the not used (no permission)\n        // delete result.devices;\n        delete result.server;\n        // check navigation permission\n        if (result.hmi.layout && result.hmi.layout.navigation.items) {\n            for (var i = result.hmi.layout.navigation.items.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n                var permission = result.hmi.layout.navigation.items[i].permission;\n                if (permission && !(permission & groups)) {\n                    result.hmi.layout.navigation.items.splice(i, 1);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        // check view item permission show / enabled\n        for (var i = 0; i < result.hmi.views.length; i++) {\n            if (result.hmi.views[i].items) {\n                for (const item of Object.values(result.hmi.views[i].items)) {\n                    if (item.property && item.property.permission) {\n                        var view = result.hmi.views[i];\n                        var mask = (item.property.permission >> 8);\n                        var show = (mask) ? mask & groups : 1;\n                        mask = (item.property.permission & 255);\n                        var enabled = (mask) ? mask & groups : 1;\n                        if (!show) {\n                            var position = view.svgcontent.indexOf(item.id);\n                            if (position >= 0) {\n                                position += item.id.length + 1;\n                                var hidetext = ' visibility=\"hidden\" ';\n                                view.svgcontent = view.svgcontent.slice(0, position) + hidetext + view.svgcontent.slice(position);\n                            }\n                        } else if (!enabled) {\n                            item.property.events = [];\n                            // disable the html controls (select, input, button)\n                            var splitted = utils.domStringSplitter(view.svgcontent, 'foreignobject', view.svgcontent.indexOf(item.id));\n                            if (splitted.tagcontent && splitted.tagcontent.length > 0) {\n                                var disabled = utils.domStringSetAttribute(splitted.tagcontent, ['select', 'input', 'button'], 'disabled');\n                                view.svgcontent = splitted.before + disabled + splitted.after;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return result;\n}\n\nfunction _mergeDefaultConfig() {\n    return new Promise(async function (resolve, reject) {\n        try {\n            if (process.env.DEVICES && typeof process.env.DEVICES === 'string') {\n                try {\n                    logger.info('project.merge-config: in progress!');\n                    var devices = JSON.parse(process.env.DEVICES);\n                    for (const device of devices) {\n                        try {\n                            // check device required\n                            if (!device || !device.id || !device.name || !device.type || !device.configs) {\n                                logger.error(`project.merge-config: DEVICES${JSON.stringify(device)} missing property!`);\n                            } else {\n                                var existDevice = data.devices[device.id];\n                                var deviceToAdd = new Device(device);\n                                if (existDevice) {\n                                    deviceToAdd.tags = existDevice.tags;\n                                }\n                                setDevice(deviceToAdd, true);\n                                logger.info(`project.merge-config: Device ${deviceToAdd.name} added!`);    \n                            }\n                        } catch (error) {\n                            logger.error(`project.merge-config: DEVICES${JSON.stringify(device)} failed! ${error}`);\n                            reject();\n                        }                            \n                    }\n                } catch (error) {\n                    logger.error(`project.merge-config: DEVICES failed! ${error}`);\n                }\n            }\n            resolve();\n        } catch (error) {\n            logger.error(`project.merge-config: failed! ${error}`);\n            reject();\n        }\n    });\n\n    function Device(device, tags) {\n        this.id = device.id;\n        this.name = device.name;\n        this.enabled = true;\n        this.type = device.type;\n        this.polling = 1000 || device.configs.requestIntervalMs;\n        this.tags = tags || {};\n flag\n    var db_daqmap;                          // Database of mapped data \n    var db_daqdata;                         // Database of data\n    var daqTagsMap = {};                    // Mapped db Tags/Nodes\n    var daqNextToken = Date.now();// Interval to split Database data\n\n    daqNextToken += (settings.daqTokenizer) ? db_daqtoken * settings.daqTokenizer : db_daqtoken * 24;\n    if === 0) {\n                _checkToArchiveDBfile(filePath);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    // define file database\n    var suffix = (daqNextToken) ? _getDateTimeSuffix(new Date()) : '';\n   // reset daq db\n        _resetDB(db_daqdata_file);\n    }\n\n    // bind database daqdata\n    _bindDaqData(db_daqdata_file).then(result => {\n        logger.info(`daqstorage.connected-to-data '${id}' ${error}`);\n        }\n    });\n\n    // bind database daqmap\n    _bindDaqMap(db_daqmap_file).then(result => {\n        logger.info(`daqstorage.connected-to-map '${db_daqmap_file}' database`, true);\n        db_daqmap = result;\n        _loadMap().then(result => {\n            logger.info(`daqstorage.load-map successful! '${id}'`, true);\n            initready = true;\n        }).catch(function (error) {\n            if (error) {\n                logger.error(`daqstorage.load-map failed! '${id}'`, true);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set function callback to get Tag/Node property and return function reference to set value\n     */\n    this.setCall = function (fncgetprop) {\n        fncGetTagProp = fncgetprop;\n        return this.addDaqValues;\n    }\n    var fncGetTagProp = null;\n\n    /**\n     * Add Daq value of Tag/Node\n     * Check if the Tag/Node is mapped otherwise first add the value to data db then check if the db is to split and to archive\n     */\n    this.addDaqValue = function (tagid, tagvalue) {\n        if (initready) {\n            if (daqTagsMap[tagid]) {\n                if (_checkDataWorking(true)) {\n                    // check if db_daqdata are bindet\n                    if (db_daqdata) {\n                        _insertTagValue(daqTagsMap[tagid].mapid, tagvalue).then(function (lastts) {\n                            // check db tokenizer after inserted\n                            if (daqNextToken && daqNextToken < lastts) {\n                                // close data DB, open and bind the new db, rename and move the closed db \n                                db_daqdata.close(function () {\n                                    var suffix = _getDateTimeSuffix(new Date());\n                                    var oldfile = db_daqdata_file;\n                                    db_daqdata_file = path.join(settings.dbDir, db_daqdata_prefix + id + '_' + suffix + '.db');\n                                    db_daqdata = null;\n                                    _bindDaqData(db_daqdata_file).then(result => {\n                                        logger.info(`daqstorage.add-daq-value _bindDaqData '${id}' database`, true);\n                                        daqNextToken += (settings.daqTimeToken) ? '${id}' ${error}`);\n                        });\n                    }\n                }\n            } else {\n                // tags is not mapped\n                var prop = fncGetTagProp(tagid);\n                if (prop && _checkMapWorking(true)) {\n                    _insertTagToMap(prop.id, prop.name, prop.type).then(function (result) {\n                        _getTagMap(prop.id, prop.name, prop.type).then(function (result) {\n                            _addTagMap(result.mapid, prop.id, prop.name);\n                        }).catch(function (error) {\n                            logger.error(`daqstorage.add-daq-value _getTagMap failed! '${id}' ${error}`);\n                        });\n                        _checkMapWorking(false);\n                    }).catch(function (error) {\n                        _checkMapWorking(false);\n                        logger.error(`daqstorage.add-daq-value _insertTagToMap failed! '${id}' ${error}`);\n                    });\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add Daq value of Tag/Node\n     * Check if the Tag/Node is mapped otherwise first add the value to data db then check if the db is to split and to archive\n     */\n    this.addDaqValues = function (tags, tagid, tagvalue) {\n        if (initready) {\n            if (db_daqdata) {\n                var addMapfnc = [];\n                var addDaqfnc = [];\n                // prepare functions\n                for (var tagid in tags) {\n                    if (!tags[tagid].daq || !tags[tagid].daq.enabled) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    if (daqTagsMap[tagid]) {\n                        addDaqfnc.push(_insertTagValue(daqTagsMap[tagid].mapid, tags[tagid].value));\n                    } else {\n                        var prop = fncGetTagProp(tagid);\n                        if (prop) {\n                            addMapfnc.push(_insertTagToMap(prop.id, prop.name, prop.type));\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                // check function to insert in map            \n                if (addMapfnc.length > 0) {\n                    Promise.all(addMapfnc).then(result => {\n                        logger.info(`daqstorage.add-daq-values _insertTagToMap '${id}' ${result}`, true);\n                        for (var idx = 0; idx < result.length; idx++) {\n                            _getTagMap(result[idx]).then(function (result) {\n                                _addTagMap(result.mapid, result.id, result.name);\n                            }).catch(function (error) {\n                                logger.error(`daqstorage.add-daq-value _getTagMap failed! '${id}' ${error}`);\n                        }\n                        _checkDataWorking(false);\n                    });\n                } \n                // check function to add daq data            \n                if (addDaqfnc.length > 0 && _checkDataWorking(true)) {\n                        Promise.all(addDaqfnc).then(result => {\n                            // check db tokenizer after inserted\n                            var lastts = 0 || result[0];\n                            if (daqNextToken && daqNextToken < lastts) {\n                                // close data DB, open and bind the new db, rename and move the closed db \n                                db_daqdata.close(function () {\n                                    var suffix = _getDateTimeSuffix(new Date());\n                                    var oldfile = db_daqdata_file;\n                                    db_daqdata_file = path.join(settings.dbDir, db_daqdata_prefix + id + '_' + suffix + '.db');\n                                    db_daqdata = null;\n                                    _bindDaqData(db_daqdata_file).then(result => {\n                                        logger.info(`daqstorage.add-daq-values '${db_daqmap_file}' database`, true);\n                                        daqNextToken += (settings.daqTimeToken) ? db_daqtoken * settings.daqTimeToken : db_daqtoken;\n                                        db_daqdata = result;\n                                        _archiveDBfile(oldfile, lastts);\n                                        _checkDataWorking(false);\n                                    }).catch(function (error) {\n                                        _checkDataWorking(false);\n                                        logger.error(`daqstorage.add-daq-values _bindDaqData failed! '${id}' ${error}`);\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return Tags/Nodes map list\n     */\n    this.getDaqMap = function () {\n        return daqTagsMap;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return array of timeserie <timestamp, value>\n     */\n    this.getDaqValue = function (tagid, fromts, tots) {\n        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n            if (daqTagsMap[tagid]) {\n                var result = [];\n                // search in current db\n                    _getTagValues(db_daqdata, daqTagsMap[tagid].mapid, fromts, tots).then(function (rows) {\n                    // search in archive\n                    var archivefiles = _getArchiveFiles(id, fromts, tots);\n                    var dbfncs = [];\n                    for (const file of archivefiles) {\n                        dbfncs.push(_bindAndGetTagValues(file, daqTagsMap[tagid].mapid, fromts, tots));\n                    }\n                    Promise.all(dbfncs).then(values => {\n                        for (const value of values) {\n                            result = result.concat(value);\n                        }\n                        result = result.concat(rows);\n                        resolve(result);\n                    }, error => {\n                        if (error.stack) {\n                            logger.error(`daqstorage.get-daq-value failed! '${id}'`);\n            return false;\n        }\n        mapworking = check;\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Used to manage the async add Tag/Node in data db (that not overloading)\n     * @param {*} check \n     */\n    var _checkDataWorking = function (check) {\n        if (check && dataworking) {\n            logger.warn(`daqstorage.data-overload! '${id}'`);\n            return false;\n        }\n        dataworking = check;\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Bind the map database by create the table if not exist\n     * @param {*} dbfile \n     */\n    function _bindDaqMap(dbfile) {\n        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n            try {\n                var db = new sqlite3.Database(dbfile, function (err) {\n                    if (err) {\n                        logger.error(`daqstorage.bind-daq-map error! '${id}' ${err}`);\n                        reject();\n                    }\n                    logger.info(`daqstorage.bind-daq-map '${dbfile}' database`, true);\n                });\n                db.serialize(function () {\n                    db.run(\"CREATE TABLE if not exists data (mapid INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, id TEXT, name TEXT, type TEXT)\", function (err) {\n                        if (err) {\n                            logger.error(`daqstorage.bind-daq-map-to-create-table error! '${id}' ${err}`);\n                            reject();\n                        } else {\n                            resolve(db);\n                        }\n                    });\n                });\n            } catch (error) {\n                reject(error);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Bind the data database by create the table if not exist\n     * @param {*} dbfile \n     */\n    function _bindDaqData(dbfile) {\n        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {\n            try {\n                var db = new sqlite3.Database(dbfile, function (err) {\n                    if (err) {\n                        logger.error(`daqstorage.bind-daq-data error! '${id}' ${err}`);\n                        reject();\n                    }\n                    logger.info(`daqstorage.bind-daq-data '${dbfile}' database`, true);\n                });\n                db.serialize(function () {\n                    db.run(\"CREATE TABLE if not exists data (dt INTEGER, id INTEGER, value TEXT)\", function (err) {\n                        if (err) {\n                            logger.error(`daqstorage.bind-daq-data-to-create-table error! '${id}' ${err}`);\n                            reject();\n                        } else {\n                            resolve(db);\n                        }\n                    });\n                });\n            } catch (error) {\n                reject(error);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Move the db file to archive folder.\n     * Open the db take the last data and rename the file with the start and last data time\n     * @param {*} dbfile \n     */\n    function _checkToArchiveDBfile(dbfile) {\n        if (dbfile.includes('-journal')) {\n            // delete pending db journal\n            fs.unlinkSync(dbfile);\n        } else {\n            _bindDaqData(dbfile).then(result => {\n                logger.info(`daqstorage.check-to-archive-db-file '${dbfile}'`, true);\n                _getLastTagValue(result).then(lastrow => {\n                    result.close(function () {\n                        // rename and move to archive\n                        if (lastrow) {\n                            var filearchived = _archiveDBfile(dbfile, lastrow.dt);\n                            logger.info(`daqstorage.check-to-archive-db-file '${filearchived}'`, true);\n                        } else {\n                            // delete void db\n                            try {\n                                fs.unlinkSync(dbfile);\n                                logger.info(`daqstorage.check-to-archive-db-file '${dbfile}' database deleted!`, true);\n                            } catch {}\n                        }\n                    });\n                }).catch(function (error) {\n                    logger.error(`daqstorage.check-to-archive-db-file error! '${id}' ${error}`);\n                });\n            }).catch(function (error) {\n                logger.error(`daqstorage.check-to-archive-db-file error! '${id}' ${error}`);\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    function _getArchiveFiles(id, fromts, tots) {\n        const archive = path.resolve(settings.dbDir, archive_folder);\n        var result = [];\n        if (fs.existsSync(archive)) {\n            for (const file of fs.readdirSync(archive)) {\n                const fromTo = _suffixToTimestamp(file);\n                if
